So What? ^9d2NlzDg

For the past 4-5 years I've followed a Daily Note first approach, which works extremely well for my meeting notes workflows ^H5evt56h

I tried PARA but the folder structure fell apart ^tZ4CWCTZ

I don't really do research, Zettelkasten had a bit too much friction for me, yet I find the ethos of Zettelkasten very compelling. ^4zoYkQBq

Back in the days... in TheBrain I started off with a Content First approach, then gravitated to a Topic First setup ^2ACXTJdo

I plan to evolve my Daily Note first approach into a Topic First setup in Obsidian. I will keep the Daily Note first approach for my work/meeting notes, but handle everything else in a Topic First way. I will also give Zettelkasten another try, feeding it from my new Daily Note first / Topic First hybrid. ^6Xm7Radn
